<span class="author db" style="margin:4px 0;">by Xinhua</span> <span class="abs db">President Xi Jinping on Thursday met here with representatives attending a ceremony commending role models with disabilities and people who have made outstanding contributions in helping the disabled.</span> 
</div>
<div class="module1" style="margin-top:15px;">
<h3><a href="http://english.qstheory.cn/2019-05/17/c_1124506581.htm" target="_blank">Xi sends congratulatory letter to World Intelligence Congress</a></h3>
<span class="author db" style="margin:4px 0;">by Xinhua</span> <span class="abs db">President Xi Jinping sent a congratulatory letter to the Third World Intelligence Congress, which opened in northern China's Tianjin municipality Thursday.</span> 
</div>
</div>

<div class="text">
<h2><a href="http://english.qstheory.cn/2019-05/08/c_1124465363.htm" target="_blank">China's iconic revolutionary base Yan'an bids farewell to poverty</a></h2>
<span class="author db" style="margin:8px 0;">by Xinhua</span> <span class="abs db">Yan'an, a former revolutionary base of the Communist Party of China (CPC), is no longer labeled "poor," as its last two impoverished counties have shaken off poverty, the Shaanxi provincial government announced Tuesday.</span> 
</div>

                    </a>
                  <p><a target="_blank" shape="rect" href="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/a/201904/08/WS5cab15c0a3104842260b4ff3.html">Beijing Miyun</a></p>
                </li>
  
              </ul>

            </div>
            <div class="yanqing_left" style="width: 600px;float: right;">
              

  <p class="topic_title"><a target="_blank" shape="rect" href="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/a/201904/03/WS5ca46404a3104842260b4365.html">A journey back to the Qing Dynasty in Beijing</a></p>
              <p class="article"><a target="_blank" shape="rect" href="https://www.chinadaily.com.cn/a/201904/03/WS5ca46404a3104842260b4365.html">Beijing’s 24th annual Spring Excursion Festival of Yuanmingyuan Ruins Park opened April 3 and will run until May 15.</a></p>

    <div class="main_art">
      <div class="lft_art" id="lft-art">
        <h1>Why dialogue is what we need in our globalized world</h1>
        <div class="info">
          <!-- 稿件 作者 来源，发布日期 -->
          <span class="info_l">
            By Hujjatullah Zia | 
          chinadaily.com.cn |
            Updated: 2019-05-18 11:33
          </span>
          <span class="info_r">
            <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/f_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/w_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/in_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/more_art.gif" /></a>
          </span>
          <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/button.js#style=-1&amp;uuid=a92f8285-36fe-4168-8f86-8e177d015e67&amp;pophcol=2&amp;lang=en"></SCRIPT>
          <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/bshareC0.js"></SCRIPT>
        </div>
        <!-- 稿件正文. -->
        <div id="Content">
          
          <figure class="image" style="display: table;"> 
 <img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/images/201905/18/5cdf7cf9a3104842e4ae43ab.jpeg" data-from="newsroom" data-mimetype="image/jpeg" id="img-5cdf7cf9a3104842e4ae43ab"> 
 <figcaption style="display: table-caption; caption-side: bottom;">
   An Asian culture carnival is held during the Conference on Dialogue of Asian Civilizations (CDAC) at the National Stadium, or the Bird's Nest, in Beijing, capital of China, May 15, 2019. [Photo by Wang Zhuangfei/China Daily] 
 </figcaption> 
</figure> 
<p>China is hosting the Conference on Dialogue of Asian Civilizations (CDAC), themed Exchanges and mutual learning among Asian civilizations and a community with a shared future, to nurture dialogue – something that eases tension and encourages inclusion.</p> 
<p>Dialogue of civilizations is essentially the inverse of a "clash of civilizations", a call for greater solidarity on the basis of recognizing cultural diversity and intercultural exchange. This dialogue suggests that the promotion of tolerance and cooperation in a climate of mutual trust and understanding are among the best guarantees of regional and global stability.</p> 
<p>In other words, one of the main objectives of the CDAC is safeguarding and promoting cultural diversity, which has been regarded as "the common heritage of humanity" and "as necessary for humankind as biodiversity is for nature" in the UNESCO Universal Declaration on Cultural Diversity.</p> 
<p>"Dialogue, before anything else, is a search for emotional contact and sincere trust," to borrow the words of former Iranian President Mohammad Khatami, who proposed the idea of dialogue among civilizations.</p> 
<p>Holding dialogue on Asian civilization will be conducive to mutual learning and mutual understanding; it will ensure harmonious interaction and cultural exchange and create the room for tolerance and peaceful coexistence between nations. That is to say, building a utopian society or a community with shared future – where all can exercise their rights and freedoms regardless of their caste, color or creed – is possible through dialogue and communication.</p> 
<p>Dialogue and communication have played essential roles for peoples of different racial, cultural, and religious backgrounds throughout history. The ancient Silk Road was a route for dialogue and communication – besides commercial exchanges – and linked some of the biggest civilizations in the world, including China and India. It has been called the "Road of Dialogue" by the UNESCO Plan.</p> 
<p>Dialogue and cultural and intellectual exchange along the ancient Silk Road contributed much to Asian civilization. Buddhism spread through the Silk Road, with Buddhist art and shrines found in the Afghan provinces of Bamyan and Logar and the Chinese provinces of Gansu and Sichuan, where I last year visited the Giant Buddha and Mount Emei Temple and Mogao Caves. Hinduism and Islam are also said to have been introduced to Indonesia and Malaysia by Silk Road traders.</p> 
<p>In our increasingly diverse societies, a zero-sum game and only-my-backyard mindset looms large, and challenges such as climate change and terrorism pose threats to the world. The mission of Asian nations in the current globalized world is to promote the "culture of dialogue". This will deepen multilateral cooperation, foster creativity in all its diversity, record human experience and aspiration, safeguard cultural heritage in all its forms, and resolve issues through communication rather than confrontation,</p> 
<p>CDAC is an invitation to "ensure harmonious interaction among people and groups with plural, varied and dynamic cultural identities as well as their willingness to live together," as it is stated in Article 2 of UNESCO Universal Declaration on Cultural Diversity, adding that "cultural pluralism is conducive to cultural exchange and to the flourishing of creative capacities that sustain public life".</p> 
<p>To enhance the global impact of Asian civilization, Asian states need to establish cultural industries and facilitate access for the endogenous cultural products of all Asian countries – especially those in developing countries and countries in transition – to the global market and international distribution networks.</p> 
<p>They further need to promote linguistic diversity in cyberspace, encourage the production and dissemination of diversified content and cultural values of Asia in the media and global information networks, formulate policies and strategies for the protection and promotion of cultural and natural heritage, and deepen communication and cultural contact between nations.</p> 
<p><em>Hujjatullah Zia is an Afghan journalist and freelance writer.</em></p>
        </div>

        <div id="div_currpage">&nbsp;&nbsp;
          
      
  
        </div>

      <div class="ce_art">
        <h1>Top 10 Chinese cities with best business environment</h1>
      </div>
      <div class="info">
        <span class="info_l">
          
         chinadaily.com.cn |
          Updated: 2019-05-20 06:40
          <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onClick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/f_art.gif" /></a>
          <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onClick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/w_art.gif" /></a>
          <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onClick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/in_art.gif" /></a>
          <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onClick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/more_art.gif" /></a>

        </span>
        <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/button.js#style=-1&amp;uuid=a92f8285-36fe-4168-8f86-8e177d015e67&amp;pophcol=2&amp;lang=en"></SCRIPT>
        <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/bshareC0.js"></SCRIPT>

        <span class="info_r"><a href="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/mobile/daily.html" target="_blank" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/app.gif" width="200" height="26" /></a></span>
      </div>

      <div class="picshow"> 
        
          
        

        
          <a class="pagestyle" shape="rect" href="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/a/201905/20/WS5ce1db41a3104842260bc827_2.html">
            <div id="apDiv1"> </div></a>
        

        <div id="Content">
          
          <figure class="image" style="display: table;"> 
 <img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/images/201905/20/5ce1db41a3104842e4ae5a50.jpeg" data-from="newsroom" data-mimetype="image/jpeg" id="img-5ce1db41a3104842e4ae5a50"> 
 <figcaption style="display: table-caption; caption-side: bottom;"></figcaption> 
</figure> 
<p>China's financial center Shanghai has the best business environment in the country, according to a report on China's urban business environment index jointly released by the China Strategic Culture Promotion Association, the China Economic Media Association, WANB Institute and YICAI Research Institute.</p> 
<p>With an index of 86.73, Shanghai topped the list of Chinese cities with the best business environment, followed by capital city Beijing at 84.63 and Shenzhen, in South China's Guangdong province, at 84.48.</p> 
<p>The report evaluates Chinese cities according to five "soft environment" indexes — technological innovation, financing, talent, culture and life — and two "hard environment" indexes, natural resources and infrastructure.</p> 
<p>Let's take a look at the 10 Chinese cities with the best business environment.</p> 

        </div>

      function is_weixin(){
        var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
        if(ua.match(/MicroMessenger/i)=="micromessenger") {
          return true;
        } else {
          return false;
        }
      }

      function copyToClipBoard() {
        var s = $("#address").val();
        if (typeof(window.clipboardData) != "undefined" &&  window.clipboardData) {
          window.clipboardData.setData("Text", s);
          alert("Copy to clipboard！"+ "\n" + s);
        } else if (typeof(navigator.userAgent) != "undefined" && navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Opera") != -1) {
          window.location = s;
        } else if (typeof(window.netscape) != "undefined" && window.netscape) {
          try {
            netscape.security.PrivilegeManager.enablePrivilege("UniversalXPConnect");
          } catch (e) {
            alert("The browser you are using does not support this replication feature, use the Ctrl+C or right mouse...");
            //alert("被浏览器拒绝！\n请在浏览器地址栏输入'about:config'并回车\n然后将'signed.applets.codebase_principal_support'设置为'true'");
          }
          var clip = Components.classes['@mozilla.org/widget/clipboard;1'].createInstance(Components.interfaces.nsIClipboard);
          if (!clip)
            return;
          var trans = Components.classes['@mozilla.org/widget/transferable;1'].createInstance(Components.interfaces.nsITransferable);
          if (!trans)
            return;
          trans.addDataFlavor('text/unicode');
          var str = new Object();
          var len = new Object();
          var str = Components.classes["@mozilla.org/supports-string;1"].createInstance(Components.interfaces.nsISupportsString);
          var copytext = s;
          str.data = copytext;
          trans.setTransferData("text/unicode", str, copytext.length * 2);
          var clipid = Components.interfaces.nsIClipboard;
          if (!clip)
            return false;
          clip.setData(trans, null, clipid.kGlobalClipboard);
        }else{
          window.prompt("Copy to clipboard: Ctrl+C, Enter", s);
        }
      }
      //]]>
    </script>

<!-- Respond.js: min/max-width media query polyfill. Remote proxy (c) Scott Jehl. MIT/GPLv2 Lic. j.mp/respondjs -->
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
	<meta charset="utf-8" />
	<title>Respond JS Proxy</title>
</head> 
<body>
	<script>
		(function () {
			var domain, css, query, getQueryString, ajax, xmlHttp;

			/*
				https://stackoverflow.com/questions/4963673/get-url-array-variables-in-javascript-jquery/4963817#4963817
			*/
			getQueryString = function() {
				var ret = {}, parts, i, p;

				parts = (document.location.toString().split("?")[1]).split("&");

				for (i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {

					p = parts[i].split("=");
					// so strings will be correctly parsed:
					p[1] = decodeURIComponent(p[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));

					if (p[0].search(/\[\]/) >= 0) { // then it"s an array
						p[0] = p[0].replace("[]", "");

						if (typeof ret[p[0]] != "object") {
							ret[p[0]] = [];
						}
						ret[p[0]].push(p[1]);
					} else {
						ret[p[0]] = p[1];
					}
				}
				return ret;
			};

			ajax = function( url, callback ) {
				var req = xmlHttp();
				if (!req){
					return;
				}
				req.open( "GET", url, true );
				req.onreadystatechange = function () {
					if ( req.readyState != 4 || req.status != 200 && req.status != 304 ){
						return;
					}
					callback( req.responseText );
				};
				if ( req.readyState == 4 ){
					return;
				}
				req.send();
			};

			//define ajax obj 
			xmlHttp = (function() {
				var xmlhttpmethod = false,
					attempts = [
						function(){ return new XMLHttpRequest(); },
						function(){ return new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP"); },
						function(){ return new ActiveXObject("MSXML2.XMLHTTP.3.0"); }
					],
					al = attempts.length;

				while( al-- ){
					try {
						xmlhttpmethod = attempts[ al ]();
					}
					catch(e) {
						continue;
					}
					break;
				}
				return function(){
					return xmlhttpmethod;
				};
			})();

			query = getQueryString();
			css = query["css"];
			domain = query["url"];

			if (css && domain) {
				ajax(css, function (response) {
					window.name = response;
					window.location.href = domain;
				});
			}
		}());
	</script>
</body>
</html>

	var email = $('#email').val();

		$('#email').focus();
		return false;
	}

	});

}

  <div class="pagedesc"><h1>Understand Your World with China-US Focus</h1>
Diving deeper into the most crucial bilateral relationship in our time. China-US Focus is one of the leading commentary journals of Sino-American relations, providing the in-depth analysis you need to understand the events and factors that contribute to the current international landscape. <br>
Based in Hong Kong, China-US Focus proudly offers our platform to commentators from around the world, providing a multitude of viewpoints on issues as they happen, allowing our readers the opportunity to form a whole and balanced opinion. A publication of the China-United States Exchange Foundation, our magazine seeks to build stronger and deeper relations between the two nations, contributing to the peace and prosperity of our time to the benefit of the world-at-large. <a id="linkmorepagedesc" href="javascript:$('#morepagedesc').show();$('#linkmorepagedesc').hide();">>>></a><br>
<div id="morepagedesc" style="display:none;"><h2>Delivering a breadth of opinion</h2>
As the global centres of power shift and the world becomes increasingly less unipolar with the ascendency of China and <a href="/tags/china-india-relations/" target="_blank">India</a>, itâs vital that people be provided with the guidance and clarification they need to understand the international landscape. China-US Focus strives to provide that. We are proud to be the only open-platform website where thought leaders from both sides of the Pacific can discuss the issues and events relevant to both countries, helping to promote a sense of cooperation and understanding between the two peoples. From commentary on all the news from China and the United States to analyses of the future of the two countryâs <a href="/foreign-policy/" target="_blank">foreign policy</a>, we provide the crucial information you need. 
Drawing on the expertise of a diverse selection of experts including former diplomats, academics and university professors, retired military figures and policy researchers and think tank representatives, we provide the range of viewpoints on the dayâs news that you need to better inform your own. Being able to consider a multitude of opinions can give you the fresh perspective and insight required to make more informed decisions in a more complex and interconnected world.<br>
<h3>Helping to explain a complex political landscape</h3>
Browse our publication today and add to your knowledge about the worldâs most important bilateral relationship.

    <div class="main_art">
      <div class="lft_art">
        <h1>
          Renminbi to remain stable, regulator says
        </h1>
        <div class="info">
          <span class="info_l">
            By CHEN JIA | 
           China Daily |
            Updated: 2019-05-20 05:34
          </span>

          <span class="info_r">
            <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_business_en/img/f_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_business_en/img/w_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_business_en/img/in_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_business_en/img/more_art.gif" /></a>
          </span>
          <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/button.js#style=-1&amp;uuid=a92f8285-36fe-4168-8f86-8e177d015e67&amp;pophcol=2&amp;lang=en"></SCRIPT>
          <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/bshareC0.js"></SCRIPT>
        </div>
        <div id="Content">
           



          <figure class="image" style="display: table;"> 
 <img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/images/201905/20/5ce1cbdea3104842e4ae59fd.jpeg" data-from="newsroom" data-mimetype="image/jpeg" id="img-5ce1cbdea3104842e4ae59fd"> 
 <figcaption style="display: table-caption; caption-side: bottom;">
   A Chinese clerk counts RMB (renminbi) yuan banknotes at a bank in Huaibei city, East China's Anhui province, 2 May 2013. [Photo/IC] 
 </figcaption> 
</figure> 
<p><strong>Central bank vice-governor voices confidence amid currency volatility</strong></p> 
<p>The monetary authority vowed to stabilize the renminbi amid escalated trade tensions, while continuing to push forward financial opening-up and protecting overseas investors' legal rights, said a senior official from the central bank on Sunday.</p> 
<p>"We have the foundation, confidence and capacity to maintain a stable foreign exchange market in China, and keep the renminbi exchange rate at a reasonably stable equilibrium," said Pan Gongsheng, vice-governor of the People's Bank of China, the central bank, said in a statement on its website.</p> 
<p>Before his pledge, the onshore renminbi rate depreciated to 6.9182 per dollar at Friday's close, the weakest level since December, and the offshore renminbi rate hit its lowest level since November. Trade talks between China and the United States recently faltered and a large amount of additional tariffs are expected to be imposed on imports from both sides.</p> 
<p>China will take necessary measures, in response to foreign exchange market fluctuations, including using a strengthened risk management system, said Pan.</p> 
<p>He also stressed that authorities would crack down on illegal activities in foreign exchange trading.</p> 
<p>"China has sufficient policy tools," said Pan, who is also director of the State Administration of Foreign Exchange, the country's foreign exchange regulator.</p> 
<p>The PBOC vice-governor also confirmed on Sunday that China will continually implement opening-up policies and improve the environment for overseas investors and protect the legal rights of foreign investors.</p> 
<p>China will further open the financial market to welcome more overseas investors in. The cross-border trade and investment will be more free and convenient, said Pan.</p> 
<p>He called China's economy stable, as the major economic indicators were within a reasonable range.</p> 
<p>In April, the National Bureau of Statistics said the purchasing managers' index for the manufacturing sector stood at 50.1, indicating expansion as the reading was above 50.</p> 
<p>The broad money supply, or M2, increased 8.5 percent year-on-year by the end of April, compared with 8.3 percent a year earlier.</p> 
<p>"The prudential monetary policy was focused on countercyclical adjustments this year, maintaining flexibility as well as ample liquidity to promote fast growth of credit and strengthened support of private and small enterprises," Pan added.</p> 
<p>The China-US trade disputes have significantly influenced the renminbi's performance, said Wang Shengzu, co-head of Investment Strategy Group Asia Goldman Sachs.</p> 
<p>But the currency is unlikely to slip out of a reasonable range, assuming there is no big shock from the trade talks, Wang said.</p> 
<p>As a sound base for a stable renminbi, "the Chinese economy has shown signs of bouncing up, shown by the faster-than-expected growth of industrial output, retail sales, and credit in the first quarter, and this means that economic activity is improving with supportive policies", said Wang.</p>
        </div>
        <!-- pc 分页 -->

    <div class="main_art">
      <div class="lft_art" id="lft-art">
        <h1>China's ex-top securities regulator under probe</h1>
        <div class="info">
          <span class="info_l">
            
          chinadaily.com.cn |
            Updated: 2019-05-20 07:57
          </span>
          <span class="info_r">
            <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/f_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/w_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/in_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//www.chinadaily.com.cn/image_e/2017/more_art.gif" /></a>
          </span>
          <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/button.js#style=-1&amp;uuid=a92f8285-36fe-4168-8f86-8e177d015e67&amp;pophcol=2&amp;lang=en" xml:space="preserve"></script>
          <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/bshareC0.js" xml:space="preserve"></script>
        </div>
        <div id="Content">
          
          <figure class="image" style="display: table;"> 
 <img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/images/201905/20/5ce1fe54a3104842e4ae6103.jpeg" data-mimetype="image/jpeg" data-from="newsroom" id="img-5ce1fe54a3104842e4ae6103"> 
 <figcaption style="display: table-caption; caption-side: bottom;">
   File photo of Liu Shiyu, former chairman of the China Securities Regulatory Commission. [Photo/VCG] 
 </figcaption> 
</figure> 
<p>Liu Shiyu, China's former top securities regulator, was under investigation for alleged violations of the law, according to a statement Sunday from the Central Commission for Discipline Inspection.</p> 
<p>Liu, who turned himself in, stepped down in January as chairman of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, a position he kept for three years before being replaced by Yi Huiman.</p> 
<p>The central commission said in the statement that Liu is cooperating with the probe.</p>
        </div>

<div class="artic-three"><!--enpproperty <articleid>1392650</articleid><date>2019-05-14 16:23:03.0</date><author></author><title>Poverty relief through musical instruments</title><keyword>Jiao Yulu,poverty,village,music,manufacture,artisan,pipa,traditional Chinese music,wood,craft</keyword><subtitle></subtitle><introtitle></introtitle><siteid>1</siteid><nodeid>50011420</nodeid><nodename>Photo</nodename><nodesearchname>en</nodesearchname>/enpproperty--><!--enpcontent-->
<div id="Content"><!--enpcontent-->
<table align="center" style="WIDTH: 100px">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="middle" valign="center">
<center><a href="content_1392650_2.htm"><img align="center" border="0" id="1144364" md5="" sourcedescription="ç¼è¾æä¾çæ¬å°æä»¶" sourcename="æ¬å°æä»¶" src="../../site1/20190514/b083fe9c59161e44cdaf05.jpeg" title=""/></a></center>

<p></p>
<p></p></td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td align="middle" valign="center">
<p align="left" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">A musical instrument made by local manufacturers at Xuchang village, Lankao county, Central China's Henan province, May 14, 2019. [LanKao Foundation for Poverty Alleviation/VCG]</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<p>At Xuchang village in Lankao county, Central China's Henan province, the paulownia trees formerly used for sand hazard prevention are now premium material to make musical instruments.</p>

<p>Recognized as the "Village of Chinese Musical Instruments", Xuchang currently boasts 82 manufacturers with an annual production value of nearly 100 million yuan ($14 million). More than 60 percent of villagers have set up family workshops. The business creates over 1,000 jobs and 52 thousand musical instruments every year.</p>

<p>Lankao county, where devoted local Party secretary in the 1960s Jiao Yulu governed, was lifted out of poverty completely in March 2017.</p>

<p>May 14 marks the 55th anniversary of Jiao's death. For decades, Chinese Communists have been called upon to follow his example to work harder and overcome difficulties. From him, cadres learn devotion to the Chinese people.</p>

      <div class="lft_art" id="lft-art">
        <h1>Musical film celebrates, unites Asian civilizations</h1>
        <div class="info">
          <span class="info_l">
            
           chinadaily.com.cn |
            Updated: 2019-05-14 19:13
          </span>
          <span class="info_r">
            <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_index_page_en/img/f_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_index_page_en/img/w_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_index_page_en/img/in_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_index_page_en/img/more_art.gif" /></a>
          </span>
          <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/button.js#style=-1&amp;uuid=a92f8285-36fe-4168-8f86-8e177d015e67&amp;pophcol=2&amp;lang=en" xml:space="preserve"></script>
          <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/bshareC0.js" xml:space="preserve"></script>
        </div>
        <div id="Content">
          
          <iframe style="max-width:850px;" id="playerFrame" width="100%" height="479px" scrolling="no" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="true" src="//v-hls.chinadaily.com.cn/player/player.html?src=//v-hls.chinadaily.com.cn/stream/605715/73328021-902c-4ebc-9adc-3f0e32a4de94/5d5abd6b-e18d-43dc-b2b4-f402984119e1_h.m3u8&amp;p=//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/images/201905/15/5cdbfa6ea3104842e4ad9e55.jpeg&amp;l=en&amp;c=5a127c23a310f9b1cd619968&amp;s=WS5cdaa2d3a3104842260bb937&amp;d=20190514191323&amp;t=Musical+film+celebrates%2C+unites+Asian+civilizations">

          </iframe>
           
          <p>A short film released in celebration of the Asian Civilization Dialogue Conference personifies unity and the riches of the continent through song.</p>
<p>Children from Pakistan, Tajikistan, Indonesia, Iran, South Korea and China proudly sing in their own languages, the lyrics depicting the traditional cultural elements of each country.</p>
<p>Images of famous natural landscapes, traditional dances, food and national costumes are united to reflect how the richness and diversity of Asian civilization can be brought together.</p>
<p>Video by: China Review Studio </p>
<p> </p>
<p> </p>
        </div>

    <div class="main_art">
      <div class="lft_art" id="lft-art">
        <h1>Skateboard competition held in Shanghai </h1>
        <div class="info">
          <span class="info_l">
            By XING YI in Shanghai | 
         chinadaily.com.cn |
            Updated: 2019-05-19 20:00
          </span>
          <span class="info_r">
            <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_sports/img/f_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_sports/img/w_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_sports/img/in_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_sports/img/more_art.gif" /></a>
          </span>
           <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/button.js#style=-1&amp;uuid=a92f8285-36fe-4168-8f86-8e177d015e67&amp;pophcol=2&amp;lang=en"></SCRIPT>
          <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/bshareC0.js"></SCRIPT>
        </div>

        <div id="Content">
          <iframe style="max-width:850px;" id="playerFrame" width="100%" height="479px" scrolling="no" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="true" src="//v-hls.chinadaily.com.cn/player/player.html?src=//v-hls.chinadaily.com.cn/stream/605715/8eeb5385-0e34-4893-a25b-35246aed63fa/63ed1659-39cc-4642-a0f9-9ddfc5c366e3_h.m3u8&amp;p=//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/images/201905/19/5ce1456da3104842e4ae5844.jpeg&amp;l=en&amp;c=59b8d012a3108c54ed7dfc6a&amp;s=WS5ce1456da3104842260bc7da&amp;d=20190519200045&amp;t=Skateboard+competition+held+in+Shanghai">

          </iframe>
          <p>Roman Pabich from the United States won first place for men while Sakura Yosozumi from Japan topped the women's group in the Vans Park Series skateboarding competition Shanghai stop on Saturday.</p>
<p>Sixteen contestants who passed the preliminaries competed in combinations of speed, style, flow, amplitude and creativity at Yangpu Riverside Hanyi Park.</p>
<p>Young athletes showed their talent in the competition: CJ Collins, 15, placed second and Brazilian Luiz Francisco, 18, secured third place in the men's group. On the women's podium, Japan's Kisa Nakamura, 18, placed second and Brazilian Yndiara Asp was third.</p>
<p>The competition will continue in Sao Paulo, Montreal and Paris-Chelles through August before the world championships in Salt Lake City in September.</p>
        </div>

    <div class="main_art">
      <div class="lft_art" id="lft-art">
        <h1>Express baggage</h1>
        <div class="info">
          <span class="info_l">
            By Xu Haoyu | 
           China Daily |
            Updated: 2019-05-18 11:47
          </span>

          <span class="info_r">
            <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_liftstyle_index_/img/f_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_liftstyle_index_/img/w_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_liftstyle_index_/img/in_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;" shape="rect"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_liftstyle_index_/img/more_art.gif" /></a>
          </span>
          <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/button.js#style=-1&amp;uuid=a92f8285-36fe-4168-8f86-8e177d015e67&amp;pophcol=2&amp;lang=en"></SCRIPT>
          <SCRIPT type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8" src="//static.bshare.cn/b/bshareC0.js"></SCRIPT>
        </div>
        <div id="Content">
          

          <figure class="image" style="display: table;"> 
 <img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/images/201905/18/5cdf8044a3104842e4ae43c1.jpeg" data-from="newsroom" data-mimetype="image/jpeg" id="img-5cdf8044a3104842e4ae43c1"> 
 <figcaption style="display: table-caption; caption-side: bottom;">
   [Photo provided to China Daily] 
 </figcaption> 
</figure> 
<p>Luxury Milanese luggage maker Valextra has launched a new flagship store in Beijing to showcase their own stylish brand of innovation and modernity, Xu Haoyu reports.</p> 
<p>After Tokyo, Shanghai, Chengdu, and most recently Hong Kong, the Italian luxury luggage and accessories brand Valextra launched its latest flagship store in Beijing.</p> 
<p>Located in Taikoo Li in the capital's Sanlitun shopping area, the Valextra Beijing space opened its doors in late March to showcase is contemporary designs and European aesthetics.</p> 
<p>The company's CEO Sara Ferrero attended the opening ceremony with London-based Milanese designer Martino Gamper, the interior designer of the new retail space.</p> 

        </div>

      <div class="lft_art" id="lft-art">
        <h1>Martin Jacques: What China will be like as a 'great power'</h1>
        <div class="info">
          <!-- 稿件 作者 来源，发布日期 -->
          <span class="info_l">
            
          chinadaily.com.cn |
            Updated: 2019-05-20 15:03
          </span>
          <span class="info_r">
            <a title="facebook" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'facebook',0);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/f_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="twitter" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'twitter',0);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/w_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="linkedin" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.share(event,'linkedin',0);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/in_art.gif" /></a>
            <a title="More" style="cursor:pointer; " onclick="javascript:bShare.more(event);return false;"><img src="//img2.chinadaily.com.cn/static/2017www_opinion/img/more_art.gif" /></a>
          </span>

          </iframe>
          <p>Editor's note: "The rise of China is one of these great historical moments of a fundamental transformation taking place in the world," said Martin Jacques, a senior fellow at Cambridge University's Department of Politics and International Studies.</p>
<p>Jacques, also the author of the global best-seller <em>What China Will Be Like As a Great Power</em>, delivered the keynote speech at the 32nd Camden Conference in Camden, Maine, US on Feb 22, 2019. Watch the full video here.</p>
